<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomeránec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нцев</a></b>)

<ol><li>бигарадия, <a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рький</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́н</a>, чинотто</li>
<li>гесперидий, севильский <a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́н</a></li></ol>
</body>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мереть.html>мере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">merétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помереть.html>помере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomerétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помирать.html>помира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ре́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 9b/c(1).      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:помирать.html>помира́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мер-</b>; суффикс: <b>-е</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a> (5157)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мести́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomestítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещать.html>помеща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place, to put, to locate, to position, to set, to bestow, to stand</li>
<li>to invest</li>
<li>to lodge, to accommodate, to put up, to settle</li>
<li>to insert, to publish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́месь</a> (21773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + a deverbal noun derived from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> ancestor of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месить.html>меси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mesítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (originally "to mix"). Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смесь.html>смесь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smesʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mixture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́месь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pómesʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́меси</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́меси</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́месей</a></b>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пометить.html>поме́тить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pométitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">помеча́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mark
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пометить.html>поме́тить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:галочка.html>га́лочкой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pométitʹ</b> gáločkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mark with a <a href = vnd.unilang:тик.html>tick</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тик.html>tick</a> off</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to date <i>(add the date)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пометить.html>поме́тил</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письмо́</a> 15-м <a href = vnd.unilang:декабрь.html>декабря́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>pométil</b> pisʹmó 15-m dekabrjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he dated the letter the 15th of December</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

serʹjózny, u vas gromádnyj talánt i, bytʹ móžet, vas ožidájet blestjáščaja búduščnostʹ, a ja neinterésnaja, ničtóžnaja dévuška, i vy sámi otlíčno znájete, što v vášej žízni ja búdu tólʹko <b>poméxoj</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You are very clever, cultivated, serious, you have immense talent, and perhaps a brilliant future awaits you, while I am an uninteresting girl of no importance, and you know very well that I should be only a <b>hindrance</b> in your life.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1940</b>,  Павел Петрович Бажов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pavel_Bazhov" class="extiw" title="w:Pavel Bazhov">Pavel Petrovich Bazhov</a>),  “Огневушка-Поскакушка  | The Dancing Fire Maid | ”, in  <cite>Морозко</cite>, Sverdlovsk |  translated as  “The Dancing Fire Maid”, in Eve Manning, transl., <cite>Malachite Casket: Tales from the Urals</cite>, Moscow, 195-, page 182:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сперва.html>сперва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круги́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ленькие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:потом.html>пото́м</a> бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> бо́льше, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сама́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подрастать.html>подраста́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ла</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:балаган.html>балага́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришёлся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помеха.html>поме́ха</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идёт</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:балаган.html>балага́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Spervá krugí málenʹkije davála, potóm bólʹše da bólʹše, i samá podrastátʹ stála. Balagán na putí prišólsja, tólʹko éto jej ne <b>poméxa</b>. Idjót, búdto balagána i net.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">First she made a small circle, then it got bigger and bigger and she began to grow too. The hut was in her way but it didn’t <b>hinder</b> her. She danced right through it as though it wasn’t there at all.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">First she made small circles, then bigger and bigger, and she herself began to grow. The hut got in her way, only it was no <b>obstacle</b> for her. She goes as if there is no hut.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1970</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>Наде́жда</a> Яковлевна Мандельштам (<a ***помечтать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помечтать.html>помечта́ть</a> (23108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mečtátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomešátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disturb, to hinder, to impede
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne éto móžet óčenʹ sílʹno <b>pomešátʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This can badly hinder me.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шнее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tebé ne <b>pomešálo</b> by sdélatʹ domášneje zadánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It would be good if you did your homework.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>е<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мый</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-помещ-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-ем</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><i>страд. прич. <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещать.html>помеща́ть</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>Была</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:созданный.html>создана</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:специальный.html>специа́льная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:установка.html>устано́вка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оптический.html>опти́ческой</a> пропускаемости поликристаллических <a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́лов</a>, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещаемый.html>помеща́емых</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:алмазный.html>алма́зными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наковальня.html>накова́льнями</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a>.<a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomeščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ний</a></b>)

<ol><li>lodgment, premise(s), room, apartment, quarters

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помилование.html>поми́лование</a> (21816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помиловать.html>поми́ловать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomílovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помилование.html>поми́лование</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomílovanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помилование.html>поми́лования</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помилование.html>поми́лования</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помилование.html>поми́лований</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pardon, mercy</li></ol>

***помин.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́н</a> (12297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́на</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>prayer for the dead, remembrance of the dead in prayer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">datʹ déneg na <b>pomín</b> duší</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">donate money for a diseased person to be mentioned in prayer</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>in expressions only</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">лёгок <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ljógok na pomíne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">talk of the devil</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i v pomíne net</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no trace/sign</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i pomínu né bylo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there was no mention, no mention was made</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поминать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a> (10274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pominátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помянуть.html>помяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember, to recall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mention
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́хом</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>pomináj</b> menjá líxom!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">remember me kindly! (<i>sometimes used when someone leaves for a very risky venture or leaves for good</i>)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pray for the health living or the repose of the soul of the dead, to commemorate</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pominátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помять.html>помя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to squeeze, to press, to wrinkle for awhile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перчатка.html>перча́тки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвечать.html>отвеча́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On stojál dólgo, <b>pominája</b> perčátki, ne znál, što otvečátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He stood for a long time, wrinkling his gloves, and did not know how to reply.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
